<s> and sir francis and captain strong for such was the style and title of sir francis's friend passed out of the hall into the reception rooms leaving the discomfited mrs <\s>
<s> blenkinsop to disappear by a side door which led to her apartments now the only habitable rooms in the long uninhabited mansion <\s>
<s> it was a place so big that no tenant could afford to live in it and sir francis and his friend walked through room after room admiring their vastness and dreary and deserted grandeur <\s>
<s> on the right of the hall door were the saloons and drawing rooms and on the other side the oak room the parlour the grand dining room the library where pen had found books in old days <\s>
<s> round three sides of the hall ran a gallery by which and corresponding passages the chief bedrooms were approached and of which many were of stately proportions and exhibited marks of splendour <\s>
<s> on the second story was a labyrinth of little discomfortable garrets destined for the attendants of the great folks who inhabited the mansion in the days when it was first built and i do not know any more cheering mark of the increased philanthropy of our own times than to contrast our domestic architecture with that of our ancestors and to see how much better servants and poor are cared for now than in times when my lord and my lady slept under gold canopies and their servants lay above them in quarters not so airy or so clean as stables are now <\s>
<s> up and down the house the two gentlemen wandered the owner of the mansion being very silent and resigned about the pleasure of possessing it whereas the captain his friend examined the premises with so much interest and eagerness that you would have thought he was the master and the other the indifferent spectator of the place <\s>
<s> i see capabilities in it capabilities in it sir cried the captain <\s>
<s> gad sir leave it to me and i'll make it the pride of the country at a small expense <\s>
<s> what a theatre we can have in the library here the curtains between the columns which divide the room <\s>
<s> what a famous room for a galop it will hold the whole shire <\s>
<s> we'll hang the morning parlour with the tapestry in your second salon in the rue de grenelle and furnish the oak room with the moyen age cabinets and the armour <\s>
<s> armour looks splendid against black oak and there's a venice glass in the quai voltaire which will suit that high mantelpiece to an inch sir <\s>
<s> the long saloon white and crimson of course the drawing room yellow satin and the little drawing room light blue with lace over hay <\s>
<s> i recollect my old governor caning me in that little room sir francis said sententiously he always hated me my old governor <\s>

<s> she's scweeching from morning till night <\s>
<s> the captain burst out laughing <\s>

<s> tatham was sitting poring over a plan of the estate and the old housekeeper had prepared a collation in honour of her lord and master <\s>
<s> then they inspected the kitchen and stables about both of which sir francis was rather interested and captain strong was for examining the gardens but the baronet said d the gardens and that sort of thing <\s>
<s> and finally he drove away from the house as unconcernedly as he had entered it and that night the people of clavering learned that sir francis clavering had paid a visit to the park and was coming to live in the county <\s>
<s> when this fact came to be known at chatteris all the folks in the place were set in commotion high church and low church half pay captains and old maids and dowagers sporting squireens of the viciniage farmers tradesmen and factory people all the population in and round about the little place <\s>
<s> the news was brought to fairoaks and received by the ladies there and by mr <\s>
<s> pen with some excitement <\s>
<s> pybus says there is a very pretty girl in the family arthur laura said who was as kind and thoughtful upon this point as women generally are a miss amory lady clavering's daughter by her first marriage <\s>
<s> of course you will fall in love with her as soon as she arrives <\s>
<s> helen cried out don't talk nonsense laura <\s>
<s> pen laughed and said well there is the young sir francis for you <\s>
<s> he is but four years old miss laura replied <\s>
<s> but i shall console myself with that handsome officer sir francis's friend <\s>
<s> he was at church last sunday in the clavering pew and his mustachios were beautiful <\s>
<s> indeed the number of sir francis's family whereof the members have all been mentioned in the above paragraphs was pretty soon known in his town and everything else as nearly as human industry and ingenuity could calculate regarding his household <\s>
<s> the park avenue and grounds were dotted now with town folks of the summer evenings who made their way up to the great house peered about the premises and criticised the improvements which were taking place there <\s>
<s> loads upon loads of furniture arrived in numberless vans from chatteris and london and numerous as the vans are there was not one but captain glanders knew what it contained and escorted the baggage up to the park house <\s>
<s> he and captain edward strong had formed an intimate acquaintance by this time <\s>
<s> the younger captain occupied those very lodgings at clavering which the peaceful smirke had previously tenanted and was deep in the good graces of madame fribsby his landlady and of the whole town indeed <\s>
<s> the captain was splendid in person and raiment fresh coloured blue eyed black whiskered broad chested athletic a slight tendency to fulness did not take away from the comeliness of his jolly figure a braver soldier never presented a broader chest to the enemy <\s>
<s> as he strode down clavering high street his hat on one side his cane clanking on the pavement or waving round him in the execution of military cuts and soldatesque manoeuvres his jolly laughter ringing through the otherwise silent street he was as welcome as sunshine to the place and a comfort to every inhabitant in it <\s>
<s> on the first market day he knew every pretty girl in the market he joked with all the women had a word with the farmers about their stock and dined at the agricultural ordinary at the clavering arms where he set them all dying with laughing by his fun and jokes <\s>
<s> tu be sure he be a vine veller tu be sure that he be was the universal opinion of the gentlemen in top boots <\s>
<s> he shook hands with a score of them as they rode out of the inn yard on their old nags waving his hat to them splendidly as he smoked his cigar in the inn gate <\s>
<s> in the course of the evening he was free of the landlady's bar knew what rent the landlord paid how many acres he farmed how much malt he put in his strong beer and whether he ever ran in a little brandy unexcised by kings from baymouth or the fishing villages along the coast <\s>
<s> he had tried to live at the great house first but it was so dull he couldn't stand it <\s>
<s> i am a creature born for society he told captain glanders <\s>

<s> blenkinsop to disappear by a side door which led to her apartments now the only habitable rooms in the long uninhabited mansion <\s>
<s> it was a place so big that no tenant could afford to live in it and sir francis and his friend walked through room after room admiring their vastness and dreary and deserted grandeur <\s>
<s> on the right of the hall door were the saloons and drawing rooms and on the other side the oak room the parlour the grand dining room the library where pen had found books in old days <\s>
<s> round three sides of the hall ran a gallery by which and corresponding passages the chief bedrooms were approached and of which many were of stately proportions and exhibited marks of splendour <\s>
<s> on the second story was a labyrinth of little discomfortable garrets destined for the attendants of the great folks who inhabited the mansion in the days when it was first built and i do not know any more cheering mark of the increased philanthropy of our own times than to contrast our domestic architecture with that of our ancestors and to see how much better servants and poor are cared for now than in times when my lord and my lady slept under gold canopies and their servants lay above them in quarters not so airy or so clean as stables are now <\s>
<s> up and down the house the two gentlemen wandered the owner of the mansion being very silent and resigned about the pleasure of possessing it whereas the captain his friend examined the premises with so much interest and eagerness that you would have thought he was the master and the other the indifferent spectator of the place <\s>
<s> i see capabilities in it capabilities in it sir cried the captain <\s>
<s> gad sir leave it to me and i'll make it the pride of the country at a small expense <\s>
<s> what a theatre we can have in the library here the curtains between the columns which divide the room <\s>
<s> what a famous room for a galop it will hold the whole shire <\s>
<s> we'll hang the morning parlour with the tapestry in your second salon in the rue de grenelle and furnish the oak room with the moyen age cabinets and the armour <\s>
<s> armour looks splendid against black oak and there's a venice glass in the quai voltaire which will suit that high mantelpiece to an inch sir <\s>
<s> the long saloon white and crimson of course the drawing room yellow satin and the little drawing room light blue with lace over hay <\s>
<s> i recollect my old governor caning me in that little room sir francis said sententiously he always hated me my old governor <\s>
<s> chintz is the dodge i suppose for my lady's rooms the suite in the landing to the south the bedroom the sitting room and the dressing room <\s>
<s> we'll throw a conservatory out over the balcony <\s>
<s> where will you have your rooms <\s>
<s> put mine in the north wing said the baronet with a yawn and out of the reach of miss amory's confounded piano <\s>
<s> i can't bear it <\s>
<s> she's scweeching from morning till night <\s>
<s> the captain burst out laughing <\s>
<s> he settled the whole further arrangements of the house in the course of their walk through it and the promenade ended they went into the steward's room now inhabited by mrs <\s>
<s> blenkinsop and where mr <\s>
<s> tatham was sitting poring over a plan of the estate and the old housekeeper had prepared a collation in honour of her lord and master <\s>
<s> then they inspected the kitchen and stables about both of which sir francis was rather interested and captain strong was for examining the gardens but the baronet said d the gardens and that sort of thing <\s>
<s> and finally he drove away from the house as unconcernedly as he had entered it and that night the people of clavering learned that sir francis clavering had paid a visit to the park and was coming to live in the county <\s>
<s> when this fact came to be known at chatteris all the folks in the place were set in commotion high church and low church half pay captains and old maids and dowagers sporting squireens of the viciniage farmers tradesmen and factory people all the population in and round about the little place <\s>
<s> the news was brought to fairoaks and received by the ladies there and by mr <\s>
<s> pen with some excitement <\s>
<s> pybus says there is a very pretty girl in the family arthur laura said who was as kind and thoughtful upon this point as women generally are a miss amory lady clavering's daughter by her first marriage <\s>
<s> of course you will fall in love with her as soon as she arrives <\s>
<s> helen cried out don't talk nonsense laura <\s>
<s> pen laughed and said well there is the young sir francis for you <\s>
<s> he is but four years old miss laura replied <\s>
<s> but i shall console myself with that handsome officer sir francis's friend <\s>
<s> he was at church last sunday in the clavering pew and his mustachios were beautiful <\s>
<s> indeed the number of sir francis's family whereof the members have all been mentioned in the above paragraphs was pretty soon known in his town and everything else as nearly as human industry and ingenuity could calculate regarding his household <\s>
<s> the park avenue and grounds were dotted now with town folks of the summer evenings who made their way up to the great house peered about the premises and criticised the improvements which were taking place there <\s>
<s> loads upon loads of furniture arrived in numberless vans from chatteris and london and numerous as the vans are there was not one but captain glanders knew what it contained and escorted the baggage up to the park house <\s>
<s> he and captain edward strong had formed an intimate acquaintance by this time <\s>
<s> the younger captain occupied those very lodgings at clavering which the peaceful smirke had previously tenanted and was deep in the good graces of madame fribsby his landlady and of the whole town indeed <\s>
<s> the captain was splendid in person and raiment fresh coloured blue eyed black whiskered broad chested athletic a slight tendency to fulness did not take away from the comeliness of his jolly figure a braver soldier never presented a broader chest to the enemy <\s>
<s> as he strode down clavering high street his hat on one side his cane clanking on the pavement or waving round him in the execution of military cuts and soldatesque manoeuvres his jolly laughter ringing through the otherwise silent street he was as welcome as sunshine to the place and a comfort to every inhabitant in it <\s>
<s> on the first market day he knew every pretty girl in the market he joked with all the women had a word with the farmers about their stock and dined at the agricultural ordinary at the clavering arms where he set them all dying with laughing by his fun and jokes <\s>
<s> tu be sure he be a vine veller tu be sure that he be was the universal opinion of the gentlemen in top boots <\s>
<s> he shook hands with a score of them as they rode out of the inn yard on their old nags waving his hat to them splendidly as he smoked his cigar in the inn gate <\s>
<s> in the course of the evening he was free of the landlady's bar knew what rent the landlord paid how many acres he farmed how much malt he put in his strong beer and whether he ever ran in a little brandy unexcised by kings from baymouth or the fishing villages along the coast <\s>
<s> he had tried to live at the great house first but it was so dull he couldn't stand it <\s>
<s> i am a creature born for society he told captain glanders <\s>
<s> i'm down here to see clavering's house set in order for between ourselves frank has no energy sir no energy he's not the chest for it sir and he threw out his own trunk as he spoke ); but i must have social intercourse <\s>
<s> blenkinsop goes to bed at seven and takes polly with her <\s>
<s> there was nobody but me and the ghost for the first two nights at the great house and i own it sir i like company <\s>
<s> most old soldiers do <\s>
<s> glanders asked strong where he had served <\s>
<s> captain strong curled his mustache and said with a laugh that the other might almost ask where he had not served <\s>
<s> i began sir as cadet of hungarian uhlans and when the war of greek independence broke out quitted that service in consequence of a quarrel with my governor and was one of seven who escaped from missolonghi and was blown up in one of botzaris's fireships at the age of seventeen <\s>
<s> i'll show you my cross of the redeemer if you'll come over to my lodgings and take a glass of grog with me captain this evening <\s>
<s> i've a few of those baubles in my desk <\s>
<s> i've the white eagle of poland skrzynecki gave it me he pronounced skrzynecki's name with wonderful accuracy and gusto upon the field of ostrolenka <\s>
<s> i was a lieutenant of the fourth regiment sir and we marched through diebitsch's lines bang thro em into prussia sir without firing a shot <\s>
<s> ah captain that was a mismanaged business <\s>
<s> i received this wound by the side of the king before oporto where he would have pounded the stock jobbing pedroites had bourmont followed my advice and i served in spain with the king's troops until the death of my dear friend zumalacarreguy when i saw the game was over and hung up my toasting iron captain <\s>
<s> alava offered me a regiment the queen's muleteros but i couldn't damme i couldn't and now sir you know ned strong the chevalier strong they call me abroad as well as he knows himself <\s>
<s> in this way almost everybody in clavering came to know ned strong <\s>

<s> and finally he drove away from the house as unconcernedly as he had entered it and that night the people of clavering learned that sir francis clavering had paid a visit to the park and was coming to live in the county <\s>
<s> when this fact came to be known at chatteris all the folks in the place were set in commotion high church and low church half pay captains and old maids and dowagers sporting squireens of the viciniage farmers tradesmen and factory people all the population in and round about the little place <\s>
<s> the news was brought to fairoaks and received by the ladies there and by mr <\s>
<s> pen with some excitement <\s>
<s> pybus says there is a very pretty girl in the family arthur laura said who was as kind and thoughtful upon this point as women generally are a miss amory lady clavering's daughter by her first marriage <\s>
<s> of course you will fall in love with her as soon as she arrives <\s>
<s> helen cried out don't talk nonsense laura <\s>
<s> pen laughed and said well there is the young sir francis for you <\s>
<s> he is but four years old miss laura replied <\s>
<s> but i shall console myself with that handsome officer sir francis's friend <\s>
<s> he was at church last sunday in the clavering pew and his mustachios were beautiful <\s>
<s> indeed the number of sir francis's family whereof the members have all been mentioned in the above paragraphs was pretty soon known in his town and everything else as nearly as human industry and ingenuity could calculate regarding his household <\s>
<s> the park avenue and grounds were dotted now with town folks of the summer evenings who made their way up to the great house peered about the premises and criticised the improvements which were taking place there <\s>
<s> loads upon loads of furniture arrived in numberless vans from chatteris and london and numerous as the vans are there was not one but captain glanders knew what it contained and escorted the baggage up to the park house <\s>
<s> he and captain edward strong had formed an intimate acquaintance by this time <\s>
<s> the younger captain occupied those very lodgings at clavering which the peaceful smirke had previously tenanted and was deep in the good graces of madame fribsby his landlady and of the whole town indeed <\s>
<s> the captain was splendid in person and raiment fresh coloured blue eyed black whiskered broad chested athletic a slight tendency to fulness did not take away from the comeliness of his jolly figure a braver soldier never presented a broader chest to the enemy <\s>
<s> as he strode down clavering high street his hat on one side his cane clanking on the pavement or waving round him in the execution of military cuts and soldatesque manoeuvres his jolly laughter ringing through the otherwise silent street he was as welcome as sunshine to the place and a comfort to every inhabitant in it <\s>
<s> on the first market day he knew every pretty girl in the market he joked with all the women had a word with the farmers about their stock and dined at the agricultural ordinary at the clavering arms where he set them all dying with laughing by his fun and jokes <\s>
<s> tu be sure he be a vine veller tu be sure that he be was the universal opinion of the gentlemen in top boots <\s>
<s> he shook hands with a score of them as they rode out of the inn yard on their old nags waving his hat to them splendidly as he smoked his cigar in the inn gate <\s>
<s> in the course of the evening he was free of the landlady's bar knew what rent the landlord paid how many acres he farmed how much malt he put in his strong beer and whether he ever ran in a little brandy unexcised by kings from baymouth or the fishing villages along the coast <\s>
<s> he had tried to live at the great house first but it was so dull he couldn't stand it <\s>
<s> i am a creature born for society he told captain glanders <\s>
<s> i'm down here to see clavering's house set in order for between ourselves frank has no energy sir no energy he's not the chest for it sir and he threw out his own trunk as he spoke ); but i must have social intercourse <\s>
<s> blenkinsop goes to bed at seven and takes polly with her <\s>
<s> there was nobody but me and the ghost for the first two nights at the great house and i own it sir i like company <\s>
<s> most old soldiers do <\s>
<s> glanders asked strong where he had served <\s>
<s> captain strong curled his mustache and said with a laugh that the other might almost ask where he had not served <\s>
<s> i began sir as cadet of hungarian uhlans and when the war of greek independence broke out quitted that service in consequence of a quarrel with my governor and was one of seven who escaped from missolonghi and was blown up in one of botzaris's fireships at the age of seventeen <\s>
<s> i'll show you my cross of the redeemer if you'll come over to my lodgings and take a glass of grog with me captain this evening <\s>
<s> i've a few of those baubles in my desk <\s>
<s> i've the white eagle of poland skrzynecki gave it me he pronounced skrzynecki's name with wonderful accuracy and gusto upon the field of ostrolenka <\s>
<s> i was a lieutenant of the fourth regiment sir and we marched through diebitsch's lines bang thro em into prussia sir without firing a shot <\s>
<s> ah captain that was a mismanaged business <\s>
<s> i received this wound by the side of the king before oporto where he would have pounded the stock jobbing pedroites had bourmont followed my advice and i served in spain with the king's troops until the death of my dear friend zumalacarreguy when i saw the game was over and hung up my toasting iron captain <\s>
<s> alava offered me a regiment the queen's muleteros but i couldn't damme i couldn't and now sir you know ned strong the chevalier strong they call me abroad as well as he knows himself <\s>
<s> in this way almost everybody in clavering came to know ned strong <\s>
<s> he told madame fribsby he told the landlord of the george he told baker at the reading rooms he told mrs <\s>
<s> little polly her aide de camp made a curtsey and several rapid bows likewise and mrs <\s>

<s> it du my poor eyes good to see one of the family once more <\s>

<s> but he burst out laughing and said you've saddled the wrong horse old lady i'm not sir francis clavering what's come to revisit the halls of my ancestors <\s>

<s> and he pointed his hand towards the pale languid gentleman who said don't be an ass ned <\s>
<s> blenkinsop i'm sir francis clavering i recollect you quite well <\s>
<s> forgot me i suppose how dy do <\s>

<s> and sir francis and captain strong for such was the style and title of sir francis's friend passed out of the hall into the reception rooms leaving the discomfited mrs <\s>
<s> blenkinsop to disappear by a side door which led to her apartments now the only habitable rooms in the long uninhabited mansion <\s>
<s> it was a place so big that no tenant could afford to live in it and sir francis and his friend walked through room after room admiring their vastness and dreary and deserted grandeur <\s>
<s> on the right of the hall door were the saloons and drawing rooms and on the other side the oak room the parlour the grand dining room the library where pen had found books in old days <\s>
<s> round three sides of the hall ran a gallery by which and corresponding passages the chief bedrooms were approached and of which many were of stately proportions and exhibited marks of splendour <\s>
<s> on the second story was a labyrinth of little discomfortable garrets destined for the attendants of the great folks who inhabited the mansion in the days when it was first built and i do not know any more cheering mark of the increased philanthropy of our own times than to contrast our domestic architecture with that of our ancestors and to see how much better servants and poor are cared for now than in times when my lord and my lady slept under gold canopies and their servants lay above them in quarters not so airy or so clean as stables are now <\s>
<s> up and down the house the two gentlemen wandered the owner of the mansion being very silent and resigned about the pleasure of possessing it whereas the captain his friend examined the premises with so much interest and eagerness that you would have thought he was the master and the other the indifferent spectator of the place <\s>
<s> i see capabilities in it capabilities in it sir cried the captain <\s>
<s> gad sir leave it to me and i'll make it the pride of the country at a small expense <\s>

<s> he had tried to live at the great house first but it was so dull he couldn't stand it <\s>
<s> i am a creature born for society he told captain glanders <\s>

<s> i began sir as cadet of hungarian uhlans and when the war of greek independence broke out quitted that service in consequence of a quarrel with my governor and was one of seven who escaped from missolonghi and was blown up in one of botzaris's fireships at the age of seventeen <\s>
<s> i'll show you my cross of the redeemer if you'll come over to my lodgings and take a glass of grog with me captain this evening <\s>
<s> i've a few of those baubles in my desk <\s>
<s> i've the white eagle of poland skrzynecki gave it me he pronounced skrzynecki's name with wonderful accuracy and gusto upon the field of ostrolenka <\s>
<s> i was a lieutenant of the fourth regiment sir and we marched through diebitsch's lines bang thro em into prussia sir without firing a shot <\s>
<s> ah captain that was a mismanaged business <\s>
<s> i received this wound by the side of the king before oporto where he would have pounded the stock jobbing pedroites had bourmont followed my advice and i served in spain with the king's troops until the death of my dear friend zumalacarreguy when i saw the game was over and hung up my toasting iron captain <\s>
<s> alava offered me a regiment the queen's muleteros but i couldn't damme i couldn't and now sir you know ned strong the chevalier strong they call me abroad as well as he knows himself <\s>
<s> in this way almost everybody in clavering came to know ned strong <\s>

<s> and sir francis and captain strong for such was the style and title of sir francis's friend passed out of the hall into the reception rooms leaving the discomfited mrs <\s>
<s> blenkinsop to disappear by a side door which led to her apartments now the only habitable rooms in the long uninhabited mansion <\s>
<s> it was a place so big that no tenant could afford to live in it and sir francis and his friend walked through room after room admiring their vastness and dreary and deserted grandeur <\s>
<s> on the right of the hall door were the saloons and drawing rooms and on the other side the oak room the parlour the grand dining room the library where pen had found books in old days <\s>
<s> round three sides of the hall ran a gallery by which and corresponding passages the chief bedrooms were approached and of which many were of stately proportions and exhibited marks of splendour <\s>
<s> on the second story was a labyrinth of little discomfortable garrets destined for the attendants of the great folks who inhabited the mansion in the days when it was first built and i do not know any more cheering mark of the increased philanthropy of our own times than to contrast our domestic architecture with that of our ancestors and to see how much better servants and poor are cared for now than in times when my lord and my lady slept under gold canopies and their servants lay above them in quarters not so airy or so clean as stables are now <\s>
<s> up and down the house the two gentlemen wandered the owner of the mansion being very silent and resigned about the pleasure of possessing it whereas the captain his friend examined the premises with so much interest and eagerness that you would have thought he was the master and the other the indifferent spectator of the place <\s>
<s> i see capabilities in it capabilities in it sir cried the captain <\s>
<s> gad sir leave it to me and i'll make it the pride of the country at a small expense <\s>
<s> what a theatre we can have in the library here the curtains between the columns which divide the room <\s>
<s> what a famous room for a galop it will hold the whole shire <\s>
<s> we'll hang the morning parlour with the tapestry in your second salon in the rue de grenelle and furnish the oak room with the moyen age cabinets and the armour <\s>

<s> the long saloon white and crimson of course the drawing room yellow satin and the little drawing room light blue with lace over hay <\s>

<s> when this fact came to be known at chatteris all the folks in the place were set in commotion high church and low church half pay captains and old maids and dowagers sporting squireens of the viciniage farmers tradesmen and factory people all the population in and round about the little place <\s>

<s> he and captain edward strong had formed an intimate acquaintance by this time <\s>
<s> the younger captain occupied those very lodgings at clavering which the peaceful smirke had previously tenanted and was deep in the good graces of madame fribsby his landlady and of the whole town indeed <\s>
<s> the captain was splendid in person and raiment fresh coloured blue eyed black whiskered broad chested athletic a slight tendency to fulness did not take away from the comeliness of his jolly figure a braver soldier never presented a broader chest to the enemy <\s>
<s> as he strode down clavering high street his hat on one side his cane clanking on the pavement or waving round him in the execution of military cuts and soldatesque manoeuvres his jolly laughter ringing through the otherwise silent street he was as welcome as sunshine to the place and a comfort to every inhabitant in it <\s>
<s> on the first market day he knew every pretty girl in the market he joked with all the women had a word with the farmers about their stock and dined at the agricultural ordinary at the clavering arms where he set them all dying with laughing by his fun and jokes <\s>

<s> and sir francis and captain strong for such was the style and title of sir francis's friend passed out of the hall into the reception rooms leaving the discomfited mrs <\s>
<s> blenkinsop to disappear by a side door which led to her apartments now the only habitable rooms in the long uninhabited mansion <\s>
<s> it was a place so big that no tenant could afford to live in it and sir francis and his friend walked through room after room admiring their vastness and dreary and deserted grandeur <\s>
<s> on the right of the hall door were the saloons and drawing rooms and on the other side the oak room the parlour the grand dining room the library where pen had found books in old days <\s>
<s> round three sides of the hall ran a gallery by which and corresponding passages the chief bedrooms were approached and of which many were of stately proportions and exhibited marks of splendour <\s>
<s> on the second story was a labyrinth of little discomfortable garrets destined for the attendants of the great folks who inhabited the mansion in the days when it was first built and i do not know any more cheering mark of the increased philanthropy of our own times than to contrast our domestic architecture with that of our ancestors and to see how much better servants and poor are cared for now than in times when my lord and my lady slept under gold canopies and their servants lay above them in quarters not so airy or so clean as stables are now <\s>
<s> up and down the house the two gentlemen wandered the owner of the mansion being very silent and resigned about the pleasure of possessing it whereas the captain his friend examined the premises with so much interest and eagerness that you would have thought he was the master and the other the indifferent spectator of the place <\s>
<s> i see capabilities in it capabilities in it sir cried the captain <\s>
<s> gad sir leave it to me and i'll make it the pride of the country at a small expense <\s>
<s> what a theatre we can have in the library here the curtains between the columns which divide the room <\s>
<s> what a famous room for a galop it will hold the whole shire <\s>
<s> we'll hang the morning parlour with the tapestry in your second salon in the rue de grenelle and furnish the oak room with the moyen age cabinets and the armour <\s>
<s> armour looks splendid against black oak and there's a venice glass in the quai voltaire which will suit that high mantelpiece to an inch sir <\s>
<s> the long saloon white and crimson of course the drawing room yellow satin and the little drawing room light blue with lace over hay <\s>

<s> she's scweeching from morning till night <\s>

<s> tatham was sitting poring over a plan of the estate and the old housekeeper had prepared a collation in honour of her lord and master <\s>
<s> then they inspected the kitchen and stables about both of which sir francis was rather interested and captain strong was for examining the gardens but the baronet said d the gardens and that sort of thing <\s>
<s> and finally he drove away from the house as unconcernedly as he had entered it and that night the people of clavering learned that sir francis clavering had paid a visit to the park and was coming to live in the county <\s>
<s> when this fact came to be known at chatteris all the folks in the place were set in commotion high church and low church half pay captains and old maids and dowagers sporting squireens of the viciniage farmers tradesmen and factory people all the population in and round about the little place <\s>
<s> the news was brought to fairoaks and received by the ladies there and by mr <\s>
<s> pen with some excitement <\s>
<s> pybus says there is a very pretty girl in the family arthur laura said who was as kind and thoughtful upon this point as women generally are a miss amory lady clavering's daughter by her first marriage <\s>
<s> of course you will fall in love with her as soon as she arrives <\s>
<s> helen cried out don't talk nonsense laura <\s>
<s> pen laughed and said well there is the young sir francis for you <\s>
<s> he is but four years old miss laura replied <\s>
<s> but i shall console myself with that handsome officer sir francis's friend <\s>
<s> he was at church last sunday in the clavering pew and his mustachios were beautiful <\s>
<s> indeed the number of sir francis's family whereof the members have all been mentioned in the above paragraphs was pretty soon known in his town and everything else as nearly as human industry and ingenuity could calculate regarding his household <\s>
<s> the park avenue and grounds were dotted now with town folks of the summer evenings who made their way up to the great house peered about the premises and criticised the improvements which were taking place there <\s>
<s> loads upon loads of furniture arrived in numberless vans from chatteris and london and numerous as the vans are there was not one but captain glanders knew what it contained and escorted the baggage up to the park house <\s>
<s> he and captain edward strong had formed an intimate acquaintance by this time <\s>
<s> the younger captain occupied those very lodgings at clavering which the peaceful smirke had previously tenanted and was deep in the good graces of madame fribsby his landlady and of the whole town indeed <\s>
<s> the captain was splendid in person and raiment fresh coloured blue eyed black whiskered broad chested athletic a slight tendency to fulness did not take away from the comeliness of his jolly figure a braver soldier never presented a broader chest to the enemy <\s>
<s> as he strode down clavering high street his hat on one side his cane clanking on the pavement or waving round him in the execution of military cuts and soldatesque manoeuvres his jolly laughter ringing through the otherwise silent street he was as welcome as sunshine to the place and a comfort to every inhabitant in it <\s>
<s> on the first market day he knew every pretty girl in the market he joked with all the women had a word with the farmers about their stock and dined at the agricultural ordinary at the clavering arms where he set them all dying with laughing by his fun and jokes <\s>
<s> tu be sure he be a vine veller tu be sure that he be was the universal opinion of the gentlemen in top boots <\s>
<s> he shook hands with a score of them as they rode out of the inn yard on their old nags waving his hat to them splendidly as he smoked his cigar in the inn gate <\s>
<s> in the course of the evening he was free of the landlady's bar knew what rent the landlord paid how many acres he farmed how much malt he put in his strong beer and whether he ever ran in a little brandy unexcised by kings from baymouth or the fishing villages along the coast <\s>
<s> he had tried to live at the great house first but it was so dull he couldn't stand it <\s>
<s> i am a creature born for society he told captain glanders <\s>
<s> i'm down here to see clavering's house set in order for between ourselves frank has no energy sir no energy he's not the chest for it sir and he threw out his own trunk as he spoke ); but i must have social intercourse <\s>

<s> ah captain that was a mismanaged business <\s>

<s> on the second story was a labyrinth of little discomfortable garrets destined for the attendants of the great folks who inhabited the mansion in the days when it was first built and i do not know any more cheering mark of the increased philanthropy of our own times than to contrast our domestic architecture with that of our ancestors and to see how much better servants and poor are cared for now than in times when my lord and my lady slept under gold canopies and their servants lay above them in quarters not so airy or so clean as stables are now <\s>
<s> up and down the house the two gentlemen wandered the owner of the mansion being very silent and resigned about the pleasure of possessing it whereas the captain his friend examined the premises with so much interest and eagerness that you would have thought he was the master and the other the indifferent spectator of the place <\s>
<s> i see capabilities in it capabilities in it sir cried the captain <\s>
<s> gad sir leave it to me and i'll make it the pride of the country at a small expense <\s>
<s> what a theatre we can have in the library here the curtains between the columns which divide the room <\s>
<s> what a famous room for a galop it will hold the whole shire <\s>
<s> we'll hang the morning parlour with the tapestry in your second salon in the rue de grenelle and furnish the oak room with the moyen age cabinets and the armour <\s>
<s> armour looks splendid against black oak and there's a venice glass in the quai voltaire which will suit that high mantelpiece to an inch sir <\s>
<s> the long saloon white and crimson of course the drawing room yellow satin and the little drawing room light blue with lace over hay <\s>
<s> i recollect my old governor caning me in that little room sir francis said sententiously he always hated me my old governor <\s>
<s> chintz is the dodge i suppose for my lady's rooms the suite in the landing to the south the bedroom the sitting room and the dressing room <\s>
<s> we'll throw a conservatory out over the balcony <\s>
<s> where will you have your rooms <\s>
<s> put mine in the north wing said the baronet with a yawn and out of the reach of miss amory's confounded piano <\s>
<s> i can't bear it <\s>
<s> she's scweeching from morning till night <\s>
<s> the captain burst out laughing <\s>
<s> he settled the whole further arrangements of the house in the course of their walk through it and the promenade ended they went into the steward's room now inhabited by mrs <\s>
<s> blenkinsop and where mr <\s>
<s> tatham was sitting poring over a plan of the estate and the old housekeeper had prepared a collation in honour of her lord and master <\s>
<s> then they inspected the kitchen and stables about both of which sir francis was rather interested and captain strong was for examining the gardens but the baronet said d the gardens and that sort of thing <\s>
<s> and finally he drove away from the house as unconcernedly as he had entered it and that night the people of clavering learned that sir francis clavering had paid a visit to the park and was coming to live in the county <\s>
<s> when this fact came to be known at chatteris all the folks in the place were set in commotion high church and low church half pay captains and old maids and dowagers sporting squireens of the viciniage farmers tradesmen and factory people all the population in and round about the little place <\s>
<s> the news was brought to fairoaks and received by the ladies there and by mr <\s>
<s> pen with some excitement <\s>
<s> pybus says there is a very pretty girl in the family arthur laura said who was as kind and thoughtful upon this point as women generally are a miss amory lady clavering's daughter by her first marriage <\s>
<s> of course you will fall in love with her as soon as she arrives <\s>
<s> helen cried out don't talk nonsense laura <\s>
<s> pen laughed and said well there is the young sir francis for you <\s>
<s> he is but four years old miss laura replied <\s>
<s> but i shall console myself with that handsome officer sir francis's friend <\s>
<s> he was at church last sunday in the clavering pew and his mustachios were beautiful <\s>
<s> indeed the number of sir francis's family whereof the members have all been mentioned in the above paragraphs was pretty soon known in his town and everything else as nearly as human industry and ingenuity could calculate regarding his household <\s>
<s> the park avenue and grounds were dotted now with town folks of the summer evenings who made their way up to the great house peered about the premises and criticised the improvements which were taking place there <\s>
<s> loads upon loads of furniture arrived in numberless vans from chatteris and london and numerous as the vans are there was not one but captain glanders knew what it contained and escorted the baggage up to the park house <\s>
<s> he and captain edward strong had formed an intimate acquaintance by this time <\s>
<s> the younger captain occupied those very lodgings at clavering which the peaceful smirke had previously tenanted and was deep in the good graces of madame fribsby his landlady and of the whole town indeed <\s>
<s> the captain was splendid in person and raiment fresh coloured blue eyed black whiskered broad chested athletic a slight tendency to fulness did not take away from the comeliness of his jolly figure a braver soldier never presented a broader chest to the enemy <\s>
<s> as he strode down clavering high street his hat on one side his cane clanking on the pavement or waving round him in the execution of military cuts and soldatesque manoeuvres his jolly laughter ringing through the otherwise silent street he was as welcome as sunshine to the place and a comfort to every inhabitant in it <\s>
<s> on the first market day he knew every pretty girl in the market he joked with all the women had a word with the farmers about their stock and dined at the agricultural ordinary at the clavering arms where he set them all dying with laughing by his fun and jokes <\s>
<s> tu be sure he be a vine veller tu be sure that he be was the universal opinion of the gentlemen in top boots <\s>
<s> he shook hands with a score of them as they rode out of the inn yard on their old nags waving his hat to them splendidly as he smoked his cigar in the inn gate <\s>
<s> in the course of the evening he was free of the landlady's bar knew what rent the landlord paid how many acres he farmed how much malt he put in his strong beer and whether he ever ran in a little brandy unexcised by kings from baymouth or the fishing villages along the coast <\s>
<s> he had tried to live at the great house first but it was so dull he couldn't stand it <\s>
<s> i am a creature born for society he told captain glanders <\s>
<s> i'm down here to see clavering's house set in order for between ourselves frank has no energy sir no energy he's not the chest for it sir and he threw out his own trunk as he spoke ); but i must have social intercourse <\s>
<s> blenkinsop goes to bed at seven and takes polly with her <\s>
<s> there was nobody but me and the ghost for the first two nights at the great house and i own it sir i like company <\s>
<s> most old soldiers do <\s>
<s> glanders asked strong where he had served <\s>
<s> captain strong curled his mustache and said with a laugh that the other might almost ask where he had not served <\s>
<s> i began sir as cadet of hungarian uhlans and when the war of greek independence broke out quitted that service in consequence of a quarrel with my governor and was one of seven who escaped from missolonghi and was blown up in one of botzaris's fireships at the age of seventeen <\s>
<s> i'll show you my cross of the redeemer if you'll come over to my lodgings and take a glass of grog with me captain this evening <\s>
<s> i've a few of those baubles in my desk <\s>
<s> i've the white eagle of poland skrzynecki gave it me he pronounced skrzynecki's name with wonderful accuracy and gusto upon the field of ostrolenka <\s>
<s> i was a lieutenant of the fourth regiment sir and we marched through diebitsch's lines bang thro em into prussia sir without firing a shot <\s>
<s> ah captain that was a mismanaged business <\s>
<s> i received this wound by the side of the king before oporto where he would have pounded the stock jobbing pedroites had bourmont followed my advice and i served in spain with the king's troops until the death of my dear friend zumalacarreguy when i saw the game was over and hung up my toasting iron captain <\s>
<s> alava offered me a regiment the queen's muleteros but i couldn't damme i couldn't and now sir you know ned strong the chevalier strong they call me abroad as well as he knows himself <\s>
<s> in this way almost everybody in clavering came to know ned strong <\s>
<s> he told madame fribsby he told the landlord of the george he told baker at the reading rooms he told mrs <\s>
<s> little polly her aide de camp made a curtsey and several rapid bows likewise and mrs <\s>
<s> blenkinsop with a great deal of emotion quavered out welcome to clavering sir francis <\s>
<s> it du my poor eyes good to see one of the family once more <\s>
<s> the speech and the greetings were all addressed to the grand gentleman in fur and braiding who wore his hat so magnificently on one side and twirled his mustachios so royally <\s>
<s> but he burst out laughing and said you've saddled the wrong horse old lady i'm not sir francis clavering what's come to revisit the halls of my ancestors <\s>

<s> and he pointed his hand towards the pale languid gentleman who said don't be an ass ned <\s>
<s> blenkinsop i'm sir francis clavering i recollect you quite well <\s>

<s> of course you will fall in love with her as soon as she arrives <\s>

<s> pen laughed and said well there is the young sir francis for you <\s>
<s> he is but four years old miss laura replied <\s>
<s> but i shall console myself with that handsome officer sir francis's friend <\s>
<s> he was at church last sunday in the clavering pew and his mustachios were beautiful <\s>
<s> indeed the number of sir francis's family whereof the members have all been mentioned in the above paragraphs was pretty soon known in his town and everything else as nearly as human industry and ingenuity could calculate regarding his household <\s>
<s> the park avenue and grounds were dotted now with town folks of the summer evenings who made their way up to the great house peered about the premises and criticised the improvements which were taking place there <\s>
<s> loads upon loads of furniture arrived in numberless vans from chatteris and london and numerous as the vans are there was not one but captain glanders knew what it contained and escorted the baggage up to the park house <\s>
<s> he and captain edward strong had formed an intimate acquaintance by this time <\s>
<s> the younger captain occupied those very lodgings at clavering which the peaceful smirke had previously tenanted and was deep in the good graces of madame fribsby his landlady and of the whole town indeed <\s>
<s> the captain was splendid in person and raiment fresh coloured blue eyed black whiskered broad chested athletic a slight tendency to fulness did not take away from the comeliness of his jolly figure a braver soldier never presented a broader chest to the enemy <\s>
<s> as he strode down clavering high street his hat on one side his cane clanking on the pavement or waving round him in the execution of military cuts and soldatesque manoeuvres his jolly laughter ringing through the otherwise silent street he was as welcome as sunshine to the place and a comfort to every inhabitant in it <\s>
<s> on the first market day he knew every pretty girl in the market he joked with all the women had a word with the farmers about their stock and dined at the agricultural ordinary at the clavering arms where he set them all dying with laughing by his fun and jokes <\s>
<s> tu be sure he be a vine veller tu be sure that he be was the universal opinion of the gentlemen in top boots <\s>
<s> he shook hands with a score of them as they rode out of the inn yard on their old nags waving his hat to them splendidly as he smoked his cigar in the inn gate <\s>
<s> in the course of the evening he was free of the landlady's bar knew what rent the landlord paid how many acres he farmed how much malt he put in his strong beer and whether he ever ran in a little brandy unexcised by kings from baymouth or the fishing villages along the coast <\s>
<s> he had tried to live at the great house first but it was so dull he couldn't stand it <\s>
<s> i am a creature born for society he told captain glanders <\s>
<s> i'm down here to see clavering's house set in order for between ourselves frank has no energy sir no energy he's not the chest for it sir and he threw out his own trunk as he spoke ); but i must have social intercourse <\s>
<s> blenkinsop goes to bed at seven and takes polly with her <\s>
<s> there was nobody but me and the ghost for the first two nights at the great house and i own it sir i like company <\s>
<s> most old soldiers do <\s>
<s> glanders asked strong where he had served <\s>
<s> captain strong curled his mustache and said with a laugh that the other might almost ask where he had not served <\s>
<s> i began sir as cadet of hungarian uhlans and when the war of greek independence broke out quitted that service in consequence of a quarrel with my governor and was one of seven who escaped from missolonghi and was blown up in one of botzaris's fireships at the age of seventeen <\s>
<s> i'll show you my cross of the redeemer if you'll come over to my lodgings and take a glass of grog with me captain this evening <\s>
<s> i've a few of those baubles in my desk <\s>
<s> i've the white eagle of poland skrzynecki gave it me he pronounced skrzynecki's name with wonderful accuracy and gusto upon the field of ostrolenka <\s>
<s> i was a lieutenant of the fourth regiment sir and we marched through diebitsch's lines bang thro em into prussia sir without firing a shot <\s>
<s> ah captain that was a mismanaged business <\s>
<s> i received this wound by the side of the king before oporto where he would have pounded the stock jobbing pedroites had bourmont followed my advice and i served in spain with the king's troops until the death of my dear friend zumalacarreguy when i saw the game was over and hung up my toasting iron captain <\s>
<s> alava offered me a regiment the queen's muleteros but i couldn't damme i couldn't and now sir you know ned strong the chevalier strong they call me abroad as well as he knows himself <\s>
<s> in this way almost everybody in clavering came to know ned strong <\s>

<s> it du my poor eyes good to see one of the family once more <\s>

<s> but he burst out laughing and said you've saddled the wrong horse old lady i'm not sir francis clavering what's come to revisit the halls of my ancestors <\s>

<s> and sir francis and captain strong for such was the style and title of sir francis's friend passed out of the hall into the reception rooms leaving the discomfited mrs <\s>
<s> blenkinsop to disappear by a side door which led to her apartments now the only habitable rooms in the long uninhabited mansion <\s>
<s> it was a place so big that no tenant could afford to live in it and sir francis and his friend walked through room after room admiring their vastness and dreary and deserted grandeur <\s>
<s> on the right of the hall door were the saloons and drawing rooms and on the other side the oak room the parlour the grand dining room the library where pen had found books in old days <\s>
<s> round three sides of the hall ran a gallery by which and corresponding passages the chief bedrooms were approached and of which many were of stately proportions and exhibited marks of splendour <\s>
<s> on the second story was a labyrinth of little discomfortable garrets destined for the attendants of the great folks who inhabited the mansion in the days when it was first built and i do not know any more cheering mark of the increased philanthropy of our own times than to contrast our domestic architecture with that of our ancestors and to see how much better servants and poor are cared for now than in times when my lord and my lady slept under gold canopies and their servants lay above them in quarters not so airy or so clean as stables are now <\s>
<s> up and down the house the two gentlemen wandered the owner of the mansion being very silent and resigned about the pleasure of possessing it whereas the captain his friend examined the premises with so much interest and eagerness that you would have thought he was the master and the other the indifferent spectator of the place <\s>
<s> i see capabilities in it capabilities in it sir cried the captain <\s>
<s> gad sir leave it to me and i'll make it the pride of the country at a small expense <\s>
<s> what a theatre we can have in the library here the curtains between the columns which divide the room <\s>
<s> what a famous room for a galop it will hold the whole shire <\s>

<s> i began sir as cadet of hungarian uhlans and when the war of greek independence broke out quitted that service in consequence of a quarrel with my governor and was one of seven who escaped from missolonghi and was blown up in one of botzaris's fireships at the age of seventeen <\s>
<s> i'll show you my cross of the redeemer if you'll come over to my lodgings and take a glass of grog with me captain this evening <\s>
<s> i've a few of those baubles in my desk <\s>
<s> i've the white eagle of poland skrzynecki gave it me he pronounced skrzynecki's name with wonderful accuracy and gusto upon the field of ostrolenka <\s>
<s> i was a lieutenant of the fourth regiment sir and we marched through diebitsch's lines bang thro em into prussia sir without firing a shot <\s>
<s> ah captain that was a mismanaged business <\s>
<s> i received this wound by the side of the king before oporto where he would have pounded the stock jobbing pedroites had bourmont followed my advice and i served in spain with the king's troops until the death of my dear friend zumalacarreguy when i saw the game was over and hung up my toasting iron captain <\s>
<s> alava offered me a regiment the queen's muleteros but i couldn't damme i couldn't and now sir you know ned strong the chevalier strong they call me abroad as well as he knows himself <\s>
<s> in this way almost everybody in clavering came to know ned strong <\s>
<s> he told madame fribsby he told the landlord of the george he told baker at the reading rooms he told mrs <\s>

<s> needn't come with us mrs <\s>
<s> what's his name you smart feed the horses and wash their mouths <\s>
<s> come along strong i know the way i was here in twenty thwee at the end of my gwandfather's time <\s>
<s> and sir francis and captain strong for such was the style and title of sir francis's friend passed out of the hall into the reception rooms leaving the discomfited mrs <\s>
<s> blenkinsop to disappear by a side door which led to her apartments now the only habitable rooms in the long uninhabited mansion <\s>
<s> it was a place so big that no tenant could afford to live in it and sir francis and his friend walked through room after room admiring their vastness and dreary and deserted grandeur <\s>
<s> on the right of the hall door were the saloons and drawing rooms and on the other side the oak room the parlour the grand dining room the library where pen had found books in old days <\s>
<s> round three sides of the hall ran a gallery by which and corresponding passages the chief bedrooms were approached and of which many were of stately proportions and exhibited marks of splendour <\s>
<s> on the second story was a labyrinth of little discomfortable garrets destined for the attendants of the great folks who inhabited the mansion in the days when it was first built and i do not know any more cheering mark of the increased philanthropy of our own times than to contrast our domestic architecture with that of our ancestors and to see how much better servants and poor are cared for now than in times when my lord and my lady slept under gold canopies and their servants lay above them in quarters not so airy or so clean as stables are now <\s>
<s> up and down the house the two gentlemen wandered the owner of the mansion being very silent and resigned about the pleasure of possessing it whereas the captain his friend examined the premises with so much interest and eagerness that you would have thought he was the master and the other the indifferent spectator of the place <\s>
<s> i see capabilities in it capabilities in it sir cried the captain <\s>
<s> gad sir leave it to me and i'll make it the pride of the country at a small expense <\s>
<s> what a theatre we can have in the library here the curtains between the columns which divide the room <\s>
<s> what a famous room for a galop it will hold the whole shire <\s>
<s> we'll hang the morning parlour with the tapestry in your second salon in the rue de grenelle and furnish the oak room with the moyen age cabinets and the armour <\s>
<s> armour looks splendid against black oak and there's a venice glass in the quai voltaire which will suit that high mantelpiece to an inch sir <\s>
<s> the long saloon white and crimson of course the drawing room yellow satin and the little drawing room light blue with lace over hay <\s>
<s> i recollect my old governor caning me in that little room sir francis said sententiously he always hated me my old governor <\s>
<s> chintz is the dodge i suppose for my lady's rooms the suite in the landing to the south the bedroom the sitting room and the dressing room <\s>
<s> we'll throw a conservatory out over the balcony <\s>
<s> where will you have your rooms <\s>
<s> put mine in the north wing said the baronet with a yawn and out of the reach of miss amory's confounded piano <\s>
<s> i can't bear it <\s>
<s> she's scweeching from morning till night <\s>
<s> the captain burst out laughing <\s>
<s> he settled the whole further arrangements of the house in the course of their walk through it and the promenade ended they went into the steward's room now inhabited by mrs <\s>
<s> blenkinsop and where mr <\s>
<s> tatham was sitting poring over a plan of the estate and the old housekeeper had prepared a collation in honour of her lord and master <\s>
<s> then they inspected the kitchen and stables about both of which sir francis was rather interested and captain strong was for examining the gardens but the baronet said d the gardens and that sort of thing <\s>
<s> and finally he drove away from the house as unconcernedly as he had entered it and that night the people of clavering learned that sir francis clavering had paid a visit to the park and was coming to live in the county <\s>
<s> when this fact came to be known at chatteris all the folks in the place were set in commotion high church and low church half pay captains and old maids and dowagers sporting squireens of the viciniage farmers tradesmen and factory people all the population in and round about the little place <\s>
<s> the news was brought to fairoaks and received by the ladies there and by mr <\s>
<s> pen with some excitement <\s>
<s> pybus says there is a very pretty girl in the family arthur laura said who was as kind and thoughtful upon this point as women generally are a miss amory lady clavering's daughter by her first marriage <\s>
<s> of course you will fall in love with her as soon as she arrives <\s>
<s> helen cried out don't talk nonsense laura <\s>
<s> pen laughed and said well there is the young sir francis for you <\s>
<s> he is but four years old miss laura replied <\s>
<s> but i shall console myself with that handsome officer sir francis's friend <\s>
<s> he was at church last sunday in the clavering pew and his mustachios were beautiful <\s>
<s> indeed the number of sir francis's family whereof the members have all been mentioned in the above paragraphs was pretty soon known in his town and everything else as nearly as human industry and ingenuity could calculate regarding his household <\s>
<s> the park avenue and grounds were dotted now with town folks of the summer evenings who made their way up to the great house peered about the premises and criticised the improvements which were taking place there <\s>
<s> loads upon loads of furniture arrived in numberless vans from chatteris and london and numerous as the vans are there was not one but captain glanders knew what it contained and escorted the baggage up to the park house <\s>
<s> he and captain edward strong had formed an intimate acquaintance by this time <\s>
<s> the younger captain occupied those very lodgings at clavering which the peaceful smirke had previously tenanted and was deep in the good graces of madame fribsby his landlady and of the whole town indeed <\s>
<s> the captain was splendid in person and raiment fresh coloured blue eyed black whiskered broad chested athletic a slight tendency to fulness did not take away from the comeliness of his jolly figure a braver soldier never presented a broader chest to the enemy <\s>
<s> as he strode down clavering high street his hat on one side his cane clanking on the pavement or waving round him in the execution of military cuts and soldatesque manoeuvres his jolly laughter ringing through the otherwise silent street he was as welcome as sunshine to the place and a comfort to every inhabitant in it <\s>
<s> on the first market day he knew every pretty girl in the market he joked with all the women had a word with the farmers about their stock and dined at the agricultural ordinary at the clavering arms where he set them all dying with laughing by his fun and jokes <\s>
<s> tu be sure he be a vine veller tu be sure that he be was the universal opinion of the gentlemen in top boots <\s>
<s> he shook hands with a score of them as they rode out of the inn yard on their old nags waving his hat to them splendidly as he smoked his cigar in the inn gate <\s>
<s> in the course of the evening he was free of the landlady's bar knew what rent the landlord paid how many acres he farmed how much malt he put in his strong beer and whether he ever ran in a little brandy unexcised by kings from baymouth or the fishing villages along the coast <\s>
<s> he had tried to live at the great house first but it was so dull he couldn't stand it <\s>
<s> i am a creature born for society he told captain glanders <\s>

<s> and sir francis and captain strong for such was the style and title of sir francis's friend passed out of the hall into the reception rooms leaving the discomfited mrs <\s>
<s> blenkinsop to disappear by a side door which led to her apartments now the only habitable rooms in the long uninhabited mansion <\s>
<s> it was a place so big that no tenant could afford to live in it and sir francis and his friend walked through room after room admiring their vastness and dreary and deserted grandeur <\s>
<s> on the right of the hall door were the saloons and drawing rooms and on the other side the oak room the parlour the grand dining room the library where pen had found books in old days <\s>
<s> round three sides of the hall ran a gallery by which and corresponding passages the chief bedrooms were approached and of which many were of stately proportions and exhibited marks of splendour <\s>
<s> on the second story was a labyrinth of little discomfortable garrets destined for the attendants of the great folks who inhabited the mansion in the days when it was first built and i do not know any more cheering mark of the increased philanthropy of our own times than to contrast our domestic architecture with that of our ancestors and to see how much better servants and poor are cared for now than in times when my lord and my lady slept under gold canopies and their servants lay above them in quarters not so airy or so clean as stables are now <\s>
<s> up and down the house the two gentlemen wandered the owner of the mansion being very silent and resigned about the pleasure of possessing it whereas the captain his friend examined the premises with so much interest and eagerness that you would have thought he was the master and the other the indifferent spectator of the place <\s>
<s> i see capabilities in it capabilities in it sir cried the captain <\s>
<s> gad sir leave it to me and i'll make it the pride of the country at a small expense <\s>
<s> what a theatre we can have in the library here the curtains between the columns which divide the room <\s>
<s> what a famous room for a galop it will hold the whole shire <\s>
<s> we'll hang the morning parlour with the tapestry in your second salon in the rue de grenelle and furnish the oak room with the moyen age cabinets and the armour <\s>
<s> armour looks splendid against black oak and there's a venice glass in the quai voltaire which will suit that high mantelpiece to an inch sir <\s>
<s> the long saloon white and crimson of course the drawing room yellow satin and the little drawing room light blue with lace over hay <\s>
<s> i recollect my old governor caning me in that little room sir francis said sententiously he always hated me my old governor <\s>
<s> chintz is the dodge i suppose for my lady's rooms the suite in the landing to the south the bedroom the sitting room and the dressing room <\s>

<s> she's scweeching from morning till night <\s>
<s> the captain burst out laughing <\s>

<s> blenkinsop and where mr <\s>
<s> tatham was sitting poring over a plan of the estate and the old housekeeper had prepared a collation in honour of her lord and master <\s>
<s> then they inspected the kitchen and stables about both of which sir francis was rather interested and captain strong was for examining the gardens but the baronet said d the gardens and that sort of thing <\s>
<s> and finally he drove away from the house as unconcernedly as he had entered it and that night the people of clavering learned that sir francis clavering had paid a visit to the park and was coming to live in the county <\s>
<s> when this fact came to be known at chatteris all the folks in the place were set in commotion high church and low church half pay captains and old maids and dowagers sporting squireens of the viciniage farmers tradesmen and factory people all the population in and round about the little place <\s>
<s> the news was brought to fairoaks and received by the ladies there and by mr <\s>
<s> pen with some excitement <\s>
<s> pybus says there is a very pretty girl in the family arthur laura said who was as kind and thoughtful upon this point as women generally are a miss amory lady clavering's daughter by her first marriage <\s>
<s> of course you will fall in love with her as soon as she arrives <\s>
<s> helen cried out don't talk nonsense laura <\s>
<s> pen laughed and said well there is the young sir francis for you <\s>
<s> he is but four years old miss laura replied <\s>
<s> but i shall console myself with that handsome officer sir francis's friend <\s>
<s> he was at church last sunday in the clavering pew and his mustachios were beautiful <\s>
<s> indeed the number of sir francis's family whereof the members have all been mentioned in the above paragraphs was pretty soon known in his town and everything else as nearly as human industry and ingenuity could calculate regarding his household <\s>
<s> the park avenue and grounds were dotted now with town folks of the summer evenings who made their way up to the great house peered about the premises and criticised the improvements which were taking place there <\s>
<s> loads upon loads of furniture arrived in numberless vans from chatteris and london and numerous as the vans are there was not one but captain glanders knew what it contained and escorted the baggage up to the park house <\s>
<s> he and captain edward strong had formed an intimate acquaintance by this time <\s>
<s> the younger captain occupied those very lodgings at clavering which the peaceful smirke had previously tenanted and was deep in the good graces of madame fribsby his landlady and of the whole town indeed <\s>
<s> the captain was splendid in person and raiment fresh coloured blue eyed black whiskered broad chested athletic a slight tendency to fulness did not take away from the comeliness of his jolly figure a braver soldier never presented a broader chest to the enemy <\s>
<s> as he strode down clavering high street his hat on one side his cane clanking on the pavement or waving round him in the execution of military cuts and soldatesque manoeuvres his jolly laughter ringing through the otherwise silent street he was as welcome as sunshine to the place and a comfort to every inhabitant in it <\s>
<s> on the first market day he knew every pretty girl in the market he joked with all the women had a word with the farmers about their stock and dined at the agricultural ordinary at the clavering arms where he set them all dying with laughing by his fun and jokes <\s>
<s> tu be sure he be a vine veller tu be sure that he be was the universal opinion of the gentlemen in top boots <\s>
<s> he shook hands with a score of them as they rode out of the inn yard on their old nags waving his hat to them splendidly as he smoked his cigar in the inn gate <\s>
<s> in the course of the evening he was free of the landlady's bar knew what rent the landlord paid how many acres he farmed how much malt he put in his strong beer and whether he ever ran in a little brandy unexcised by kings from baymouth or the fishing villages along the coast <\s>
<s> he had tried to live at the great house first but it was so dull he couldn't stand it <\s>
<s> i am a creature born for society he told captain glanders <\s>
<s> i'm down here to see clavering's house set in order for between ourselves frank has no energy sir no energy he's not the chest for it sir and he threw out his own trunk as he spoke ); but i must have social intercourse <\s>
<s> blenkinsop goes to bed at seven and takes polly with her <\s>
<s> there was nobody but me and the ghost for the first two nights at the great house and i own it sir i like company <\s>
<s> most old soldiers do <\s>
<s> glanders asked strong where he had served <\s>
<s> captain strong curled his mustache and said with a laugh that the other might almost ask where he had not served <\s>
<s> i began sir as cadet of hungarian uhlans and when the war of greek independence broke out quitted that service in consequence of a quarrel with my governor and was one of seven who escaped from missolonghi and was blown up in one of botzaris's fireships at the age of seventeen <\s>
<s> i'll show you my cross of the redeemer if you'll come over to my lodgings and take a glass of grog with me captain this evening <\s>
<s> i've a few of those baubles in my desk <\s>
<s> i've the white eagle of poland skrzynecki gave it me he pronounced skrzynecki's name with wonderful accuracy and gusto upon the field of ostrolenka <\s>
<s> i was a lieutenant of the fourth regiment sir and we marched through diebitsch's lines bang thro em into prussia sir without firing a shot <\s>
<s> ah captain that was a mismanaged business <\s>
<s> i received this wound by the side of the king before oporto where he would have pounded the stock jobbing pedroites had bourmont followed my advice and i served in spain with the king's troops until the death of my dear friend zumalacarreguy when i saw the game was over and hung up my toasting iron captain <\s>
<s> alava offered me a regiment the queen's muleteros but i couldn't damme i couldn't and now sir you know ned strong the chevalier strong they call me abroad as well as he knows himself <\s>

<s> when this fact came to be known at chatteris all the folks in the place were set in commotion high church and low church half pay captains and old maids and dowagers sporting squireens of the viciniage farmers tradesmen and factory people all the population in and round about the little place <\s>

<s> but i shall console myself with that handsome officer sir francis's friend <\s>
<s> he was at church last sunday in the clavering pew and his mustachios were beautiful <\s>
<s> indeed the number of sir francis's family whereof the members have all been mentioned in the above paragraphs was pretty soon known in his town and everything else as nearly as human industry and ingenuity could calculate regarding his household <\s>
<s> the park avenue and grounds were dotted now with town folks of the summer evenings who made their way up to the great house peered about the premises and criticised the improvements which were taking place there <\s>
<s> loads upon loads of furniture arrived in numberless vans from chatteris and london and numerous as the vans are there was not one but captain glanders knew what it contained and escorted the baggage up to the park house <\s>
<s> he and captain edward strong had formed an intimate acquaintance by this time <\s>
<s> the younger captain occupied those very lodgings at clavering which the peaceful smirke had previously tenanted and was deep in the good graces of madame fribsby his landlady and of the whole town indeed <\s>
<s> the captain was splendid in person and raiment fresh coloured blue eyed black whiskered broad chested athletic a slight tendency to fulness did not take away from the comeliness of his jolly figure a braver soldier never presented a broader chest to the enemy <\s>
<s> as he strode down clavering high street his hat on one side his cane clanking on the pavement or waving round him in the execution of military cuts and soldatesque manoeuvres his jolly laughter ringing through the otherwise silent street he was as welcome as sunshine to the place and a comfort to every inhabitant in it <\s>
<s> on the first market day he knew every pretty girl in the market he joked with all the women had a word with the farmers about their stock and dined at the agricultural ordinary at the clavering arms where he set them all dying with laughing by his fun and jokes <\s>
<s> tu be sure he be a vine veller tu be sure that he be was the universal opinion of the gentlemen in top boots <\s>
<s> he shook hands with a score of them as they rode out of the inn yard on their old nags waving his hat to them splendidly as he smoked his cigar in the inn gate <\s>
<s> in the course of the evening he was free of the landlady's bar knew what rent the landlord paid how many acres he farmed how much malt he put in his strong beer and whether he ever ran in a little brandy unexcised by kings from baymouth or the fishing villages along the coast <\s>
<s> he had tried to live at the great house first but it was so dull he couldn't stand it <\s>
<s> i am a creature born for society he told captain glanders <\s>

<s> i began sir as cadet of hungarian uhlans and when the war of greek independence broke out quitted that service in consequence of a quarrel with my governor and was one of seven who escaped from missolonghi and was blown up in one of botzaris's fireships at the age of seventeen <\s>
<s> i'll show you my cross of the redeemer if you'll come over to my lodgings and take a glass of grog with me captain this evening <\s>
<s> i've a few of those baubles in my desk <\s>
<s> i've the white eagle of poland skrzynecki gave it me he pronounced skrzynecki's name with wonderful accuracy and gusto upon the field of ostrolenka <\s>
<s> i was a lieutenant of the fourth regiment sir and we marched through diebitsch's lines bang thro em into prussia sir without firing a shot <\s>
<s> ah captain that was a mismanaged business <\s>
<s> i received this wound by the side of the king before oporto where he would have pounded the stock jobbing pedroites had bourmont followed my advice and i served in spain with the king's troops until the death of my dear friend zumalacarreguy when i saw the game was over and hung up my toasting iron captain <\s>
<s> alava offered me a regiment the queen's muleteros but i couldn't damme i couldn't and now sir you know ned strong the chevalier strong they call me abroad as well as he knows himself <\s>

<s> blenkinsop to disappear by a side door which led to her apartments now the only habitable rooms in the long uninhabited mansion <\s>
<s> it was a place so big that no tenant could afford to live in it and sir francis and his friend walked through room after room admiring their vastness and dreary and deserted grandeur <\s>
<s> on the right of the hall door were the saloons and drawing rooms and on the other side the oak room the parlour the grand dining room the library where pen had found books in old days <\s>
<s> round three sides of the hall ran a gallery by which and corresponding passages the chief bedrooms were approached and of which many were of stately proportions and exhibited marks of splendour <\s>
<s> on the second story was a labyrinth of little discomfortable garrets destined for the attendants of the great folks who inhabited the mansion in the days when it was first built and i do not know any more cheering mark of the increased philanthropy of our own times than to contrast our domestic architecture with that of our ancestors and to see how much better servants and poor are cared for now than in times when my lord and my lady slept under gold canopies and their servants lay above them in quarters not so airy or so clean as stables are now <\s>
